 The court said that the police is meant for the work of the common man, not just those who have doctoral degrees in Urdu or Persian
 peeth ne dilli police se kaha, "atyadhik lachchhedaar bhashaa, jinka arth shabdkosh main dhundhna pade, kaa istemaal nahin karnaa chahie

 (exiaar) baari bharkam shabd kii jagah aasaan bhashaa kaa istemaal hona chahie
 People need to know what has been written
 yah angreji ke istemaal par bhi lagu hota he
 Do not use heavy words

 The summer season no longer bothers the people of Basni village of Nagaur
 vahaan ke log to balki daawa karte hai ki unke gaanv mempine ke paniki samasya paidaa ho hi nahin sakati
 In fact, the traditional drinking water source of Basni, there is so much water in Gordhan Pond that by the next rain the needs of the people will be fulfilled with fun
 talab ke panika yahaan aisa pukhta or behatar prabandhan kiya gaya he, jo ek sookhe pradesh main jal sangrakshan ke achche khaase sabak kii tarah he
 This village understood the importance of water only in 1984
 un dinon talab main paaltu pashuon kaa deraa jamaa rahata tha
 The result: water rot, dirt and odor
 gaanv ke gharghar main chamadi kaa khatarnaak naru rog failane laga, jo ki sadate pani main panape ek paraseete se paidaa hota he
 The situation became distressing for drinking water too
 bade buudhon ne talab ke kinare baithkar vichaar kiya or nagauri kaumi fund naam kii cameti gathit kii
 Committee Chairman Haji Mohammad Kasam Kashmiri says, "instead of stumbling across the Dardar, we thought of extracting solutions from the pond itself
" '' cameti ne sabase pehle talab kii khudaai karwaakar uski charadivari bana di
 Due to this, water started to remain clean
 lekin gaanv ke ek varg kaa is safasuthare pani par ekadhikaar sa ho gaya
 What should the poor do To get water for everyone, first of all Rs 3,000 on the pond
 kii tankhwaah par ek chaukeedaar niyukt kiya gaya
 In addition coupons were printed for 4,000 families of the village
 maheene kii pehali taarikh ko coupon baante jate hai
 11 coupons per family
 ek coupon main ek tanker pani
 There are 10-12 tankers for supply
 coupon bhi pani kii uplabdhta dekhakar die jate
 a coupon in three months in the summer season
 yah vyavastha aaraam se chalane lagi
 Meanwhile, many people got complaints that they were given 4 coupons in the year but the neighbor got five
 samasya pair failaati, usase pehle hi kushal prabandhan kaa parichay dete hue cameti ne iskaa niraakaran kar liya
 Ration cards were made for all families
 isamen pani die jane vaale maheene ke saamne or us maheene ke coupon donon par mohar lagaai jane lagi
 Now the record of who got how much water is recorded in both the committee's register and the family's ration card
 tanker vaale manamaani na karen, iske liye unhen hidaayat di gai
 130 rupees for carrying water to any corner of the village
 talab ke chaukeedaar, rashan, coupon or safasafai ke liye gaanv waalon ke alaava un logon kaa sahyog liya jaataa he, jo gaanv ke baahar vyavsaay karte hai
 Tough measures were also taken against water thieves
 ek baar chaukeedaar se mileebhagat kar tanker vaala bina coupon ke hi pani liye ja rahaa tha
 The villagers caught him and paid Rs 2,200
 jurmaane ke saath pani bharne ke liye us par hameshaa ke liye pabandi laga di
 The watchman was also removed
 talab kaa pani bhavishyamen kam na pade or na hi pani kii aavak kam ho, iske liye bhi cameti ke logon ne duuradrushti apanaai
 Treasurer Shaukat Ali says, "the committee recently bought 20 bighas of land, for Angor (ie water way)
 sarkari record main bhi ise isi naam se darj karvaa diya gaya he
 "for 25 years no water crisis has arisen in Basni village
 aavak kaa rasta ban jane ke baad aage bhi shaayad hi aisi naubat aae
 On April 2, 8 people died in Madhya Pradesh in violence during Bharat Bandh, Dalits took to the streets across the country
 naaraazgi 1989 main bane kanoon ko kathith taur par kamjor karne ko lekar thi
 When NDTV investigated the FIR with Ground Zero, 6 Dalits were among those who died, 6 days passed but the accused are still out of the grip of the police
 bhind ke mehagaanv main 2 april ko band ke dauraan hinsa kaa tandav gwalior se lagbhag dedh ghante kii duuri par based mehagaanv main do dalit ladakon 22 saal ke pradeep or 15 saal ke akaash jatav ko goli lagi
 Pradeep did a diploma from ITI, Gwalior, was looking for a job
 pradarshnakariyon ke saath wo mehagaanv main tha jab use goli maari gai
 According to the FIR, Sonu, Monu and Ballu Rathore are accused, all upper castes who fired from the roof, these three are also accused of Akash's death
 15 saal kaa akaash bazaar se sabji kharidne gaya tha, ghar ai to use goli lagane kii khabar
 The shadow of the father arose long ago
 maa akaash ko afasar bananaa chaahati thim

 The family members of each deceased say that the Savarnas opened fire
